<Rate>5<//Rate><Text>Enrolling in martial arts classes was something that I had been interested in but, unfortunately; could not find the time.  After retiring, I went about researching an appropriate facility and found that Lockhart's Karate Academy met my requirements.  I encouraged my wife to join me in these classes since she is only 4' 11" tall and I wanted her to be able to protect herself in all scenarios.

We feel very fortunate to have found this Karate studio as we have now been members for over a year now.  Both Master Lockhart and his daughter Ms. Lockhart are exceptional instructors.  They instill discipline, respect, and fun into their training curricula.

Last week we attended our first in-house tournament and it's really amazing to witness how confident the young students are.  We were impressed at the progression and skill level that some of these kids exhibited.

It's important to note that these classes are not just for children.  In fact, I believe that this type of education is just as important as one ages since the classes provide both physical as well as mental exercise.  My wife and I were both in our fifties when we began training with Master Lockhart.  In the beginning we were complete beginners as we tried to maintain balance during the warm-up kicks.  We are now at the orange belt level and look forward to progressing through the advanced belt levels.

Lockhart's Karate Academy has my highest recommendation.<//Text>< pics>

We have had a great experience at this studio. The instructors are all knowledgeable, kind and have appropriate expectations of our children. Both our kids thoroughly enjoy their classes and instructors, and look forward to each session. Dan Lockhart is especially great with the kids. He knows them, understands them, and speaks with them in a way they understand. I have seen many instructors or coaches in other activities who won't let children attempt something or continue to work toward something because they think they can't do it. Master Lockhart has high expectations of these kids and encourages them to push themselves; as a result my children have gained confidence, resilience and grit. I also truly appreciate the candor of the instructors; if a child does not try or does not do something well, they don't try to make it sound pretty - they will identify if it's not good - but on the other hand, if a child succeeds, tries hard, or is doing well, they will absolutely make it known. In a culture where my children get trophies just for showing up, it is a rare find to have someone identify the not-so-good and celebrate the true victories.< /Review>

<Gmap_id>0x809b1aac27feb975:0xa035d61912e900bc<//Gmap_id>< review>
Quite possibly the worst customer service experience I have ever had. The service department and level of customer centricity, communication, empathy, and ability to fulfill contractual obligations of providing a loaner, was completely absent. Appointment was scheduled 5 days in advance to have our brand new Ford Transit passenger wagon's brake lines checked as we had a slow leak. Upon arrival we were informed that they do not have a loaner for our family, even though we were sure to purchase that as part of the extended warranty package, but they would also have to keep the vehicle for an extended period of time (overnight or longer) in order to get to it as they were "busy". I would expect that any new vehicle having issues like this would garner immediate attention especially with an appointment being scheduled. They provided my wife with no options to get home and provided sub par communication as she wandered around with three kids 6 and under. Once they actually checked the vehicle, they confirmed the brake lines were loose and needed to be tightened. 4.5 hours after our appointment, we received our vehicle and left for home. Once we jumped back into the van, assuming all was fixed, all dash lights came on and every warning started to not only hit the dashboard, but also the Ford Pass application. The service manager, Mark Harris, not only showed a complete lack of respect for the situation he created with his service department, but took a condescending tone towards my wife who was emotionally distraught as she was back there with 3 little kids and trying to get to our older boy's little league baseball game. They refused her service and Mark refused to have someone from the service garage come out to look and see what was going on. Knowing the impact this has on our schedule as we were in their earlier, Mark continued to belittle my wife and say he was sorry we have 5 kids, sorry we were missing the baseball game, and sorry this will likely impact our trip at the end of this week. I hope Mark Harris learns the meaning of empathy and customer support as he is apparently a leader in the service department at Auburn Ford. We will be taking this issue directly to Ford.  The only Auburn Ford team member that was empathetic and wanted to help was Denise and I would like to personally thank her for trying to support my wife in that moment. Mark, James, & Kim need to do a better job of understanding the impact on a large family or ANYONE losing their brand new vehicle, and offer solutions, not condescending remarks on the impact their poor service had on our day and possible week ahead. We will be taking our Ford vehicle to Roseville Future Ford as once my wife was refused service, she was left stranded on the side of the freeway and had to wait 2.5 hours for a tow truck big enough for the Transit. Future Ford Lincoln of Roseville is receiving our Transit this evening to resolve the issue that was created by the Auburn Ford team. Future Ford Lincoln of Roseville has already agreed to look at our vehicle first thing in the morning, and also provide us with a loaner that will fit our family. I cannot recommend the Ford service center at the Auburn location. We purchased our vehicle at Folsom Lake Ford and had an incredible experience with the team there. The Auburn FORD service center is a disappointment across the board. Save yourself the time and effort. Mark Harris, it is important for you to know that having a large family is our choice, and I do not need your condescending tone towards my wife. Something tells me that if  I was there you would've had a different tone. You should treat ALL with respect. Maybe it was our large family or my wife dealing with the issue, either way it is a lesson I hope you learn as I promise you I will make all in the area aware of how you treat members of the community.</review>

< review>
BEWARE!!!  This place is a RIPOFF!  I bought a new Ford reman engine for my truck from Auburn Ford.  After the install, I had an engine code that would not go away.  I took it into the service department for their diagnosis.  I was told that the fuel pickup / sender and the fuel pump would need to be replaced (these parts are not covered under the engine warranty).  The cost for the repair would be almost $1900.  I had consulted with the mechanic and told him that i had just removed the fuel tank pickup, disassembled it and cleaned the filters and that the fuel pump was replaces just last year.  I am a professional mechanic and performed these procedures.  After my own further inspection I had found that the fuel pressure was very low and was the possible cause of the engine code.  I went ahead and replaced the fuel pump again with a factory unit per their recommendation.  Still low fuel pressure.  Upon my further inspection I located the fuel pressure regulator and disassembled it.  I took the fuel pressure regulator spring  and stretched it out from 1 1/4 in. to 1 5/8 in. and reinstalled.  The fuel pressure instantly went from 30 psi at idle (previously causing the engine code) to 60 psi at idle (much closer to where it should be). After a test drive, the engine code never returned.  This spring was a part of the new replacement engine I had just installed. The repair that was recommended by this shop would never have solved this problem.  I replaced the fuel pressure regulator spring (cost was $24.95) with a new one and the truck runs great.  Not only was this problem misdiagnosed  but I was charged $147 for it!  I also replaced the fuel pump that was not at all defective and that was $455.  I took my own time to solve the issue that should have been covered under warranty.  The service manager, James Brown, told me there was nothing he was going to do about it!  End of story.</review>

I had an oil leak on my 2016 F150 eco-boost that was covered under warranty at Auburn Ford. It was a great experience that included a recall repair that I wasn't aware of, (I purchased the vehicle used). By the way, my truck is fantastic, I really couldn't be happier with the decision to buy a Ford.

No problem got an appointment a couple of weeks out.
Went there this morning arriving early and was surprised to find out that it is a big deal to diagnose a small localized oil leak.
I was not informed that I would need to wait "up to 5 hours" and maybe longer for this to be looked at and diagnosed or I could leave it. I thought (silly me) that when the service writer said yes we don't have anything going on that day and since it is a perceived "come back", I would roll in, they would get it up on the lift and look at it, maybe add some dye to the oil and send me down the road with an appointment in the future for the repair.
No accommodation was made or even considered.
